| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **7.1 Target metric for base year** | C7.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution assessed its in-scope financial activities at the segment or sub-asset class or business line level using the following categories defined under subcriterion C7: "In transition": Counterparties that are on a science-based pathway to net-zero; "Climate solutions": Activities that are necessary for the economy-wide transition to net-zero; "Net-zero state": Counterparties that have reached zero or near-zero emissions levels; "Not aligned": Counterparties that are not targeting a net-zero transition (Not aligned means that the application yields no match with any of the climate-alignment categories); "Not assessed": No information on the counterparty available (yet). | Provision of the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool as evidence of the climate-alignment calculations per in-scope financial activity (Tables 2.1-2.5). |
| **7.2 Portfolio climate alignment calculation** | C7.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution calculated its climate-alignment as the percentage share (%) of total in-scope financial exposure that is categorized as "in transition," "climate solutions," or "net-zero state" — referred to as FINZ.Metric.2 – per financial activity. | Provision of the climate-alignment assessment per in-scope financial activity in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool (Tables 2.1-2.5). |
| **7.3 Portfolio climate alignment calculation level** | C7.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution calculated the climate-alignment of its financial exposure at the segment level, or at the sub-asset class or business line level as per Tables 1.1-1.5 in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Provision the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool as evidence of the base year assessment of climate alignment (Tables 2.1-2.5). Supporting evidence summing to the calculations of portfolio counterparties classified as "in transition" and "climate solutions" — an excel sheet per each category, adding up to the totals reported in the FINZ tool with the following headings: The sector; Segment and asset class per Tables 1.1-1.5 of the FINZ standard; Alignment methodology/taxonomy used (from the FINZ implementation list); Achievement/score/category of counterparty. |
| **7.4 Not assessed financial activities** | C7.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution did not use the "not assessed" category for activities in segments A and B (as per Tables 1.1-1.5 in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard), which would represent a non-conformance with FINZ-C7. | Provision of the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool as evidence of the climate-alignment calculations per in-scope financial activity (Tables 2.1-2.5). |
| **7.5 Rationale for "non assessed" sub-asset classes** | C7.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | If the financial institution calculated its climate-alignment and categorized an activity as "not assessed" in segment C or D, the financial institution provided a rationale for categorizing activities as "not assessed." | Disclosure in the FINZ submission form of the activities categorized as "not assessed" in segment C or D (2.7.1). Provision in the FINZ submission form of the rationale for categorizing activities as "not assessed" (2.7.2). |
| **7.6 Portfolio assessment - methodology** | C7.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution used climate-alignment methodologies in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard Provisional Implementation List (or tools that only use those climate-alignment methodologies) or used sector metrics (via a benchmark divergence assessment) to classify counterparties. | Provision of methodologies used in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target information). |
| **7.7 Portfolio assessment - data sources** | C7.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution submitted the data source(s) used in the base-year assessment of its financial activities. | Provision of data source(s) used for the climate-alignment target in the FINZ submission form (section 3. Portfolio Target information). |

### Section 2.4: Financial Exposure Assessment

#### FINZ-C8 — Exposure Assessment

*Financial institutions shall provide an assessment of their financial exposure to clean energy relative to fossil fuel in the base year and commit to assess and publish their deforestation exposure by 2030 at the latest.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **8.1 Clean energy–to–fossil fuel financial exposure ratio** | C8.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution calculated its clean energy–to–fossil fuel financial exposure in terms of both absolute exposure amounts and the ratio for each in-scope financial activity type. | Fossil fuel exposure per financial activity type in FINZ submission form Table 2 (2.8.3). Fossil fuel exposure in FINZ submission form (2.8.3) matches the fossil fuel exposure in SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool (Tables 2.1 - 2.5). Clean energy exposure per financial activity type in the FINZ submission form Table 2 (2.8.4). |
| **8.2 Definition of fossil fuel and clean energy exposures** | C8.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution calculated the clean energy–to–fossil fuel financial exposure ratio based on the following specifications: Fossil fuel exposure: All in-scope financial activities in the fossil fuel sector as specified in Table 2 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard; Clean energy exposure: All in-scope financial activities in the clean energy sector (solar, wind, hydropower, nuclear, geothermal, bioenergy from biowaste and hydrogen produced from renewable energy sources—only as fossil fuel replacement in industrial processes), including generation, storage, transmission and distribution infrastructure. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution used the definitions stated in FINZ-C8.1 to calculate its fossil fuel and clean energy exposures (2.8.1 - 2.8.2). |
| **8.3 Exposure to permanent decommissioning of fossil fuel production activities and capacity** | C8.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | All in-scope financial activities in the fossil fuel sector dedicated to permanent decommissioning (without replacement) of fossil fuel production activities and capacity have been disclosed separately and not included in the clean energy–to–fossil fuel financial exposure ratio. | Disclosure in the FINZ submission form of the FI's exposure in the fossil fuel sector dedicated to permanent decommissioning of fossil fuel production activities and capacity per in-scope financial activities (2.8.5). |
| **8.4 Commitment on deforestation exposure transparency** | C8.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution committed to assess and publish the amount of its deforestation exposure, as defined below: Amount of in-scope activities provided to portfolio entities that are linked to, at a minimum, the loss of natural forest as a result of: (1) conversion to agriculture or other non-forest land use; (2) conversion to a tree plantation; or (3) severe and sustained degradation, stemming from any critical deforestation-linked commodities, as specified in the Annex A of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | At initial validation: confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution committed to assess and publish the amount of its deforestation exposure covering at least the definition in the description and critical deforestation-linked commodities specified in Annex A of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard (1.5.3.1). At renewal validation: evidence that the financial institution assessed and published the amount of deforestation exposure, in line with the definition in the description. |
| **8.5 Deforestation exposure commitment time frame** | C8.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution committed to assess and publish the amount of its deforestation exposure within two years after validation or by 2030 at the latest. | At initial validation: confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution committed to publish the deforestation exposure within the indicated time frame in FINZ-C8.2 (1.5.2). At renewal validation: evidence that the financial institution published its deforestation exposure within two years of the previous validation or by 2030 at the latest. |
| **8.6 Annual disclosure commitment** | C8.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution committed to continue to assess and publish the amount of its deforestation exposure annually after initial disclosure. | At initial validation: confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution committed to continue assessing and publishing its deforestation exposure annually after initial disclosure (1.5.2). At renewal validation: evidence that the financial institution published its deforestation exposure annually after initial disclosure (if applicable). |
| **8.7 Public disclosure of definitions, methodologies, metrics, and approach** | C8.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution committed to include in its public disclosures: (i) The definition of deforestation, that can go beyond the minimum as defined in FINZ-C8.2; (ii) The definition of "significant deforestation exposure" for the purposes of FINZ-C10 (using a percentage or absolute amount); (iii) The methodologies and metrics for tracking deforestation (including a cutoff date in the past); (iv) And the approach and frequency of public reporting. | At initial validation: confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution committed to include in its public disclosures for deforestation – definitions, methodologies, metrics, approach and frequency of public reporting (1.5.3.1. - 1.5.3.4.). At renewal validation: evidence that the financial institution included all the elements listed in the description in its deforestation exposure disclosures. |
| **8.6 Target language for deforestation exemption** | C8.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | (Only applicable if, after performing the exposure assessment, the financial institution did not have deforestation exposure). The financial institution committed to publish the following exemption language: "[Financial institution name] does not have applicable deforestation exposure and commits to annually assess and publicly disclose its deforestation exposure beginning in [year]." | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution assessed its deforestation exposure (1.5.1). Confirmation that the financial institution does not have deforestation exposure (1.5.1.1). Confirmation that the financial institution agrees to publish the exemption target language for deforestation (1.5.1.2). The target year is provided (1.5.1.3). The exemption target language for deforestation is provided in the FINZ submission form section 5. Target Language. |
| **8.7 Target language for fossil fuel exemption** | C8.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | (Only applicable if after performing the exposure assessment, the financial institution did not have fossil fuel exposure). The financial institution committed to publish the exemption language found in FINZ-C8, specifically in C8.3. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution agrees to publish the exemption target language for fossil fuel (1.4.7). The exemption target language for fossil fuel is provided in the FINZ submission form section 5. Target Language. |

### Chapter 3: POLICIES AND TARGET SETTING

### Section 3.1: Policies

#### FINZ-C9 — Fossil Fuel Transition Policy

*Financial institutions shall publish a policy that addresses their new financial activities in the fossil fuel sector.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **9.1 Fossil fuel transition policy applicability** | C9.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | Prior to initial validation, the financial institution published a policy that addressed new applicable financial activities in the fossil fuel sector. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution published a fossil fuel transition policy that is publicly available (1.4.1.1). Provision of a hyperlink to the FI's fossil fuel transition policy in the FINZ submission form (1.4.1.2 - 1.4.1.3). |
| **9.2 Fossil fuel transition policy applicability** | C9.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The fossil fuel transition policy included the definitions of coal, oil and gas projects and companies used (e.g., how they were determined to be in-scope against an industry classification system or approved list). The definitions in the policy at least included the value chain activities listed in Table 2 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard (and as relevant to a financial institution's portfolio). | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the fossil fuel transition policy is aligned with the definitions as per FINZ-C9.1 and Table 2 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard (1.4.2). |
| **9.3 Fossil fuel transition policy applicability** | C9.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution's fossil fuel transition policy used the term "applicable financial activities" to refer to in-scope financial activities and the use of any optional exclusions that are permitted under the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. The policy also contained explanation(s) about the use of any such optional exclusions, which include: Financial activities dedicated to the permanent decommissioning (without replacement) of production activities and capacity; Investments through advisory mandates in AMI; Financial activities dedicated to abating fossil fuel projects and infrastructure with carbon capture with at least 90%-95% capture rates and durable storage that does not support enhanced oil recovery or any other processes that enable continued fossil fuel extraction and production capacity development; Financial activities required by national laws or regulations (This only refers to new applicable financial activities that are explicitly required by published laws and regulations, e.g., a law requires financial institutions to insure a specific project). | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the policy included the minimum requirements as specified in the description (1.4.3.1). If any exclusions are used, confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the explanations were included in the fossil fuel transition policy (1.4.3.2). |
| **9.4 Fossil fuel transition policy minimum requirements for coal** | C9.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | Within its fossil fuel transition policy, the financial institution committed to the immediate cessation of new applicable financial activities provided to projects and companies involved in new coal expansion activities: New coal expansion activities covered with this commitment are defined as: new coal mines, extensions or expansions of existing coal mines, and new unabated coal-fired power plants that would require a Final Investment Decision after the FI's fossil fuel transition policy publication date; AND this commitment applies to new financial activities with a known use of proceeds (e.g., coal project finance/insurance) as well as an unknown use of proceeds (e.g., general-purpose finance/insurance to coal companies). | Indication in the FINZ submission form whether the financial institution has financial activities in the coal sector or not (1.4.4.1). If the financial institution has financial activities in the coal sector, confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the policy includes the minimum requirements as specified in the description (1.4.4.2 - 1.4.4.6). |
| **9.5 Fossil fuel transition policy minimum requirements for oil and gas** | C9.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | Within its fossil fuel transition policy, the financial institution committed to the immediate cessation of new applicable financial activities provided to projects involved in new oil and gas expansion activities: New oil and gas expansion activities covered in this commitment are defined as new upstream oil and gas projects (i.e., exploration, extraction, and the development or expansion of oil and gas fields) and new liquefied natural gas (LNG) infrastructure that would require a Final Investment Decision after the financial institution's fossil fuel transition policy publication date. This is inclusive of all LNG-related infrastructure (e.g., new import and export terminals, LNG carriers, liquid to gas, gas to liquid facilities, regasification units, and associated compression, processing, and storage equipment required throughout the LNG value chain). This commitment applies to new applicable financial activities with a known use of proceeds (e.g., oil and gas project finance/insurance) only. | Indication in the FINZ submission form whether the financial institution has provided financial activities to oil and gas projects and new liquefied natural gas (LNG) infrastructure or not (1.4.5.1). If the financial institution has provided financial activities to oil and gas projects and new LNG infrastructure, confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the policy includes the minimum requirements as specified in the description (1.4.5.2 - 1.4.5.4). |
| **9.6 Fossil fuel transition policy minimum requirements for oil and gas** | C9.4 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | Within its fossil fuel transition policy, the financial institution committed to the immediate cessation, or by 2030 at the latest, of new applicable financial activities provided to companies involved in new oil and gas expansion activities: New oil and gas expansion activities covered in this commitment are defined as new upstream oil and gas projects and new LNG infrastructure that would require a Final Investment Decision after 2030; This commitment applies to new applicable financial activities with an unknown use of proceeds (e.g., general-purpose finance/insurance to fossil fuel companies) only; The commitment within the policy clearly indicates the intended time frame to cease new general-purpose finance/insurance, and is valid as of the fossil fuel transition policy publication date, or by no later than 2030. | Indication in the FINZ submission form whether the financial institution has financial activities related to oil and gas companies (1.4.6.1). If the financial institution has financial activities related to oil and gas companies, confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the policy includes the minimum requirements as specified in the description (1.4.6.2 - 1.4.6.6). |

#### FINZ-C10 — No-Deforestation

*When significant, financial institutions shall publish an engagement plan to address deforestation in their portfolios.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **10.1 Public engagement plan for addressing deforestation** | C10.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Renewal Validation | The financial institution published an engagement plan for addressing deforestation, if it identified significant deforestation exposure in its portfolio (as per FINZ-C8). The engagement plan contains the following information: An outline of the financial institution's strategy and a timeline of action for addressing deforestation; Public disclosure on progress on the engagement plan following FINZ-C18. | Hyperlink to the FI's engagement plan if significant deforestation exposure is found during the near-term target time frame containing the information detailed in the description. |

### Section 3.2: Target Setting

#### FINZ-C11 — Non-Portfolio Targets

*Financial institutions shall set near- and long-term targets for their operational scope 1 and 2 emissions, and where applicable, scope 3 categories 1-14 emissions, in accordance with the most recently applicable criteria in the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard and/or SBTi Sector Standards.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **11.1 Non-portfolio related emissions target** | FINZ-C11 | Scope 1 and 2 — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set scope 1 and 2 targets in accordance with the most recently applicable criteria in the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard and/or SBTi Sector Standards. The financial institution shall comply with the criteria applicable to scope 1 and 2 near-term and long-term targets among the SBTi Criteria Assessment Indicator (NT-C1 to NT-C28 and NZ-C1 to NZ-C37). | The financial institution has provided all the information (e.g. GHG inventory, target(s) information, target(s) language) in the FINZ submission form (4. Non-Portfolio Targets). Provision of the SBTi Corporate Near-Term and Net-Zero Target-Setting Tools for scope 1 and 2 targets. If applicable, the financial institution reported exclusions from scope 1 and 2 emissions in Table 4.5 in the FINZ submission form. If applicable, the financial institution reported biogenic emissions and removals from bioenergy feedstocks in its scope 1 and 2 emissions in Table 4.6 in the FINZ submission form. Provision of all relevant supporting documents to verify conformance with the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard. |
| **11.2 Non-portfolio long-term target time frame** | FINZ-C11 | Scope 1 and 2 / Scope 3 categories 1-14 — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set long-term targets with a time frame of up to 2050. | Provision of the non-portfolio long-term target years within a time frame of up to 2050 in the FINZ submission form (4. Non-Portfolio Targets). |
| **11.3 Non-portfolio related emissions target** | C11.1 | Scope 3 categories 1-14 — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | If the financial institution derives less than 95% of revenue from financial activities, the financial institution has set scope 3 targets for categories 1 to 14 in accordance with the most recently applicable criteria in the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard and/or SBTi Sector Standards, with the difference that near-term targets have a time frame of up to five years. The financial institution shall comply with the criteria applicable for scope 3 near-term and long-term targets among the SBTi Criteria Assessment Indicator (NT-C1 to NT-C28 and NZ-C1 to NZ-C37). | Disclosure of the percentage of revenue derived from financial activities in the FINZ submission form (4.4.1). The financial institution specified in the FINZ submission form the activities relevant across its scope 3 inventory and provided a complete inventory for all the relevant activities (4.5.1 – 4.5.14 and Tables 4.3.1-4.3.14). If applicable, provision of the SBTi Corporate Near-Term and Net-Zero Target-Setting tools for scope 3 target(s). If applicable, the financial institution reported exclusions from scope 3 emissions in Table 4.5 in the FINZ submission form. If applicable, the financial institution reported biogenic emissions and removals from bioenergy feedstocks in its scope 1 and 2 emissions in Table 4.6 in the FINZ submission form. Provision of all relevant supporting documents to verify conformance with the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard. If applicable, the financial institution has provided the Buildings Target-Setting Tool and Buildings Annex for its buildings target(s). |
| **11.4 Non-portfolio near-term target time frame** | C11.2 | Scope 1 and 2 / Scope 3 categories 1-14 — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set near-term targets with a time frame of up to five years. | Provision of the non-portfolio near-term target years within a time frame of up to five years from the submission date in the FINZ submission form (4. Non-Portfolio Targets). |
| **11.5 Non-portfolio near-term target year** | C11.2 | Scope 1 and 2 / Scope 3 categories 1-14 — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution used the same target year for all near-term targets. | Provision of a consistent target year for all non-portfolio near-term targets for scope 1 and 2 and, if applicable, scope 3 categories 1-14 targets in the FINZ submission form (4. Non-Portfolio Targets). |

#### FINZ-C12 — Portfolio Near-Term Targets

*Financial institutions shall set one or multiple near-term targets for each in-scope financial activity (i.e., scope 3, category 15 emissions) using any of the eligible target metrics and target-setting methods.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **12.1 Portfolio (financial activity) near-term target** | FINZ-C12 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set one or multiple near-term targets for each in-scope financial activity. | Each in-scope financial activity is covered and target(s) information is completed in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target Information). |
| **12.2 Near-term target metric** | C12.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution used any of the eligible climate-alignment metric or sector metrics, for its near-term target(s) in accordance with the options allowed in Table 3 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Disclosure of the financial institution's near term target(s) metrics used in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool. |
| **12.3 Consistent near-term target metric** | C12.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution confirmed that the same target metric(s) will be used consistently throughout the target period for each near-term target set. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the same target metrics will be used consistently throughout the target period for each near-term target set (6.1.1). |
| **12.4 Near-term target coverage** | C12.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set near-term targets covering at least 67% of activities in segments A, B, C and D (in terms of financial or GHG emissions exposure). A full (i.e., all in-scope exposure) inventory for scope 3, category 15 emissions has been provided if the 67% threshold is calculated in terms of GHG emissions. | Financial exposure OR GHG emissions per in-scope financial activity in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool. Target coverage per near-term target set in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool. Confirmation in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool of the share of segments A+B+C and D covered with targets by in-scope financial activity type. |
| **12.5 Near-term target coverage** | C12.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution included 100% of activities in segments A, B, and C as a minimum in the coverage of its near-term targets. | Target coverage in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool. Confirmation in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool of the share of segments A+B+C covered with targets by in-scope financial activity type. If applicable, provision of the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the coverage of the FI's sector target(s). |
| **12.6 Near-term target ambition** | C12.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set near-term targets that meet or exceed the level of ambition specified in Table 3 for portfolio climate-alignment targets and, for sector targets, the target-setting methods specified in Table 4.3 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. The financial institution used climate-alignment methodologies in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard Provisional Implementation List (or tools that only use those climate-alignment methodologies) or used sector metrics (via a benchmark divergence assessment) to set targets. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the portfolio climate-alignment assessment provided per in-scope financial activity and segment. Disclosure of the FI's portfolio climate-alignment target ambitions in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target Information). If applicable, provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the sector-specific target calculations. If applicable, disclosure of the FI's sector-specific target ambitions in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target Information). |
| **12.7 Progress to date** | C12.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS / Scope 1, 2, 3 (categories 1-14) — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The targets submitted for validation have not been achieved by the date they are submitted to SBTi Services for validation. In such cases, the financial institution established a target that meets or exceeds the ambition level required in the subsequent milestone year, as specified in Table 3 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Provision of the SBTi Corporate Near-Term and Net-Zero Target-Setting tools for scope 1 and 2 targets, and, if applicable, scope 3 targets. Provision of the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool. |
| **12.8 Near-term target year** | C12.4 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set near-term targets with a target year that is within five years from the calendar year the targets are submitted to the SBTi for an official validation. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the target years of the FI's portfolio climate-alignment targets and, if applicable, sector targets. |
| **12.9 Near-term target year** | C12.4 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution used the same target year for all near-term targets. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the target years of the FI's portfolio climate-alignment targets and, if applicable, sector targets. |
| **12.10 Near-term target aggregation** | C12.5 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution followed the level of target aggregation as specified below: Targets have to be disclosed on an aggregate level and following the break-down by segments per financial activity in Table 3. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the target(s) at the financial activity and segment level. Provision in the Target Language section in the FINZ submission form of the portfolio target language as per Annex B in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. |

*FINZ-C13 — Portfolio long-term targets: Financial institutions shall set one long-term net-zero-alignment target for each in-scope financial activity.*

| **13.1 Portfolio (financial activity) long-term target** | FINZ-C13 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set one long term target(s) for each of its in-scope financial activity. | Disclosure of the FI's long-term portfolio climate-alignment target ambitions in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target Information). |
| **13.2 Long-term target metric** | C13.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution used the climate-alignment metric (FINZ.Metric.2 as set out in Table 4.1 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard) for setting its long-term targets. | Disclosure of the FI's long-term target metric in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target Information) in accordance with Table 4.1 in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. |
| **13.3 Long-term target coverage** | C13.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set long-term targets covering 100% of activities in segments A, B, C, and D as listed in Tables 1.1-1.5 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the coverage of the FI's portfolio climate-alignment targets. Confirmation in the SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool of the share of segments A+B+C and D covered with targets by in-scope financial activity type. |
| **13.4 Long-term target ambition** | C13.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set long-term targets with an ambition to reach at least 95% of financial activities to counterparties operating at the required net-zero state, as defined in Table 4.2 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. The financial institution used climate-alignment methodologies listed in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard Provisional Implementation List (or tools that only use those climate-alignment methodologies). | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the portfolio climate-alignment assessment provided per in-scope financial activity and segment. Disclosure of the FI's portfolio climate-alignment target ambitions in the FINZ submission form (3. Portfolio Target Information). |
| **13.5 Long-term target year** | C13.4 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set long-term targets with a target year of 2050 or earlier and consistent with the net-zero target year commitment. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the target years of the FI's portfolio climate-alignment targets. Provision of the FI's target year for its net-zero commitment (1.1.1). |
| **13.6 Long-term target aggregation** | C13.5 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has set long-term targets at the aggregate level and for each relevant segment in Table 3 of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Provision of SBTi FINZ Target-Setting Tool with the target(s) at the financial activity level. Provision in the Target Language section in the FINZ submission form of the portfolio target language as per Annex B in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. |

### Section 3.3: Neutralization and the financial institution net-zero state

#### FINZ-C14 — Financial institutions' net-zero state

*Financial institutions shall ensure that counterparties in their portfolio achieve a state of net-zero emissions by the net-zero target year, involving the reduction of their scope 1, 2 and 3 emissions to zero or residual levels\*, and the neutralization of any residual emissions.*

*\*Emissions refers to "Gross GHG emissions attributable to all in-scope financial activities" in line with FINZ Metric.1 in Table 4.1. Residual levels for counterparties are defined per sector net-zero benchmark levels as detailed in Table 4.3 and/or the latest SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **14.1 Neutralization and Financial institution net-zero state** | FINZ-C14 and C14.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Net-zero target year | The financial institution ensured that the counterparties in its portfolio achieved a state of net-zero emissions by the net-zero target year, involving the reduction of their scope 1, 2 and 3 emissions to zero or residual levels, and the neutralization of any residual emissions in accordance with the most recently applicable criteria in the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard. | At the net-zero target year: evidence that the counterparties in FI's portfolio achieved the net-zero emissions state in line with the requirements listed in the description and with the most recently applicable criteria in the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard. |

### Section 3.4: Communicating policies and targets

#### FINZ-C15 — Communicating policies and targets

*Financial institutions shall transparently communicate policies and targets in accordance with the requirements specified in this Standard.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **15.1 Financial institution target language** | C15.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA / Scope 1, 2 and 3 categories 1-14 (if applicable) — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution followed the target language template set out in Annex B in the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Provision of the scope 1 and 2, and, if applicable, scope 3 categories 1-14 target language in accordance with the SBTi Corporate Net-Zero Standard in the FINZ submission form (5. Target Language). Provision in the FINZ submission form (5. Target Language) of the portfolio target language in accordance with Annex B in the Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. Provision in the FINZ submission form (5. Target Language) of the deforestation exposure and fossil fuel transition policy language in accordance with Annex B in the Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. |
| **15.2 Publication of approved targets** | C15.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution agreed to publish its targets in the SBTi Target Dashboard within six months of receiving a positive validation decision. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that targets will be published within six months of the approval date (6.2.2). |
| **15.3 Communication of approved targets** | C15.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA / Scope 1, 2, and 3 categories 1-14 (if applicable) — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution's published target language is consistent with the validated target formulation. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will use the same target language approved by the SBTi in its own communications (6.2.1). |
| **15.4 Targets unpublished after 6 months** | C15.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA / Scope 1, and 2, and 3 categories 1-14 (if applicable) — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution agreed that, if its validated targets are not published within six months of receiving a positive validation decision, then these targets are no longer valid and the financial institution will have to undergo the validation process again in order to publish targets. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that financial institution's targets not published within six months of a positive validation decision are no longer valid (6.2.3). |

### Section 3.5: Target recalculation and validity

#### FINZ-C16 — Triggered target recalculation

*Financial institutions shall commit to recalculation based on significant organizational changes and adherence to SBTi validation cycles and policies.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **16.1 SBTi validation cycles and policies** | C16.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS / Scope 1, 2 and 3 categories 1-14 (if applicable) — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution committed to recalculate its target(s) based on the SBTi validation cycles and policies. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will recalculate its target(s) based on the SBTi validation cycles and policies (6.3.1). |
| **16.2 Changes triggering recalculation** | C16.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS / Scope 1, 2 and 3 categories 1-14 (if applicable) — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution committed to recalculate its target(s) and submit them for revalidation if there is a significant change that could compromise existing validated target(s). A target recalculation for financial institutions is triggered by the following changes: Significant change in scope 1 and scope 2 emissions, as well as in any scope 3, categories 1-14 emissions that are covered by target(s), from a financial institution's base year emissions. Significant changes in company structure and activities (e.g., acquisition, divestiture, merger, insourcing, or outsourcing). Other significant changes to projections or assumptions used in setting the target(s). Significant adjustments to the base year assessment, data sources or calculation methodologies, or changes in data used to set targets (e.g., discovery of significant errors or multiple cumulative errors that are collectively significant). | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will recalculate its target(s) and submit them for revalidation if required (6.3.2). |
| **16.3 Targets recalculation** | C16.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS — Initial Validation | The financial institution agreed to follow the SBTi's significance threshold for recalculation, which is defined as a cumulative change of 5% or more in an organization's total base year emissions (tCO₂e). | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution has a base year emissions recalculation policy (6.3.4). |

## Chapter 4: ASSESSING AND COMMUNICATING PROGRESS

### Section 4.1: Reporting

#### FINZ-C17 — Reporting

*Financial institutions shall commit to publicly report progress against targets on an annual basis.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **17.1 Public disclosure of GHG emissions inventory** | C17.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has committed to separately and publicly report the information outlined below for each in-scope financial activity on an annual basis: Gross GHG emissions inventory in FINZ-C6 for segments A, B and C, as well as the GHG accounting methodology, assumptions, data sources and data quality scores of the underlying data used, as per FINZ-C6.6, with separate reporting of: Scope 1+2 and scope 1+2+3 portfolio-level GHG emissions, separately. Carbon removals, carbon credits, and avoided emissions, (as relevant). Fossil fuel-related emissions, and as data quality allows, methane emissions (CH₄) within that. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will adhere to the public reporting requirements listed as bullet points in FINZ C17.1 (6.4.1. - 6.4.1.5). |
| **17.2 Public disclosure of portfolio climate-alignment** | C17.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has committed to separately and publicly report on its climate-alignment and sector metric assessment (if relevant) established in FINZ-C7, including a breakdown of climate-alignment methodologies used for the climate-alignment assessment for each in-scope financial activity on an annual basis. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will publicly report on its portfolio climate-alignment and, if relevant, sector metric assessment (6.4.4). |
| **17.3 Full GHG inventory commitment** | C17.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has committed to implement a progressive increase in scope and quality to a full gross portfolio emissions inventory and a full climate-alignment assessment (i.e., without a "not assessed" category) for all in-scope financial activities (i.e., segments A, B, C and D) every year from 2030 (at the latest). | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution is committed to progressively improving the scope and quality of its emissions inventory and climate-alignment assessment (6.4.3). |
| **17.4 Public disclosure of clean energy to fossil fuel exposure** | C17.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has committed to separately and publicly report its clean energy–to–fossil fuel financial exposure ratio, per FINZ-C8, including the corresponding financial exposure amounts. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will report on its clean energy–to–fossil fuel financial exposure ratio and corresponding financial exposure amounts (6.4.5 and 6.4.7). |
| **17.5 Public disclosure of deforestation exposure** | C17.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has committed to separately and publicly report its deforestation exposure, in line with FINZ-C8. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will separately and publicly report its deforestation exposure (6.4.6). |
| **17.6 Annual reporting commitment** | C17.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution has committed to start the annual progress reporting in the year following validation. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution will report progress against published targets annually (6.4.8). |

### Section 4.2: Progress assessment and target renewal

#### FINZ-C18 — Progress and target renewal

*Financial institutions shall determine progress against their validated target(s) at the end of their near-term target time frame and, when relevant, establish new target(s) and submit them for validation.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **18.1 Progress against target(s) disclosure** | C18.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Renewal Validation | The financial institution assessed and publicly disclosed progress against its validated target(s) no later than 12 months after the near-term target time frame elapsed. | At renewal validation: provision of evidence the assessment and disclosure of progress against validated target(s) in the requested time frame. |
| **18.2 SBTi Criteria version for recalculation** | C18.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Renewal Validation | If applicable, the financial institution submitted new targets for validation addressing the remaining gap between the progress at the end of its near-term target time frame and the next target cycle or the next-zero target year. | At renewal validation: Submission of new targets for validation, if applicable. |

## Chapter 5: SBTi CLAIMS

#### FINZ-C19 — SBTi claims

*Financial institutions shall ensure all claims are accurate, transparent, verifiable and compatible with the criteria in this Standard and SBTi policies.*

| Indicator Number | Reference | Applicability | Criteria Assessment Indicator | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-----------------|-----------|--------------|-------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| **19.1 SBTi claims adherence** | C19.1 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution adhered, at all times, to all relevant SBTi policies and procedures, including, but not limited to, SBTi Communications Guidance, Claims, Brand, and Validation policies. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that the financial institution adheres and will adhere to all relevant SBTi policies and procedures (6.5.2). |
| **19.2 SBTi claim wording** | C19.2 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | Any claim made by the financial institution accurately communicated the conformance status of the financial institution by using the appropriate claims wording, as stipulated in the target language in Annex B of the SBTi Financial Institutions Net-Zero Standard. | Confirmation that any claims communicate and will communicate the accurate status of the financial institution and follow SBTi requirements (6.5.4). |
| **19.3 SBTi claim wording** | C19.3 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | The financial institution ensured that all claims are accurate, verifiable, and transparent, avoiding language that may mislead stakeholders or misrepresent the FI's climate-related ambition, progress, or performance. | Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that any claims are and will be in accordance with SBTi requirements (6.5.3). If the financial institution has made any claims, provision of the hyperlink to the public SBTi claims (6.5.1). |
| **19.4 SBTi claim content** | C19.4 | LND, AOI, AMI, INS, CMA — Initial Validation / Renewal Validation | All claim content was fully substantiated with relevant and verifiable evidence, which was accessible for transparency purposes to the SBTi, third parties and/or regulatory bodies upon request. | Provision of the hyperlink to any public SBTi claims in the FINZ submission form (6.5.1). Confirmation in the FINZ submission form that all claim content is and will be fully substantiated with relevant and verifiable evidence (6.5.5). |

---

## FOREST, LAND AND AGRICULTURE (FLAG) SECTOR

### Table 9. FLAG Sector Criteria Assessment Table

**FLAG C1 — Companies required to set FLAG targets:** The SBTi requires companies that meet either of the following two criteria to set a FLAG target:

i) Companies from the following FLAG-designated sectors are required to set FLAG targets: Forest and Paper Products–Forestry, Timber, Pulp and Paper, Rubber. Food Production: Agricultural Production. Food Production: Animal Source. Food and Beverage Processing. Food and Staples Retailing. Tobacco.

ii) Companies with FLAG-related emissions that total 20% or more of overall emissions across scopes 1, 2 and 3.

Companies that meet i) or ii) above and are in the process of setting science-based targets for SBTi validation or updating existing targets shall also set FLAG targets. Companies that meet i) or ii) above and have already set an SBTi science-based target without a FLAG target shall set a FLAG target at the latest as part of their mandatory five-year review submission, and should set it as soon as possible. *In line with the SBTi Mandatory Five-Year Review Guidance.*

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **1.1 FLAG-designated sectors** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies from the following FLAG-designated sectors are required to set FLAG targets: Forest and Paper Products: Forestry, Timber, Pulp and Paper, Rubber. Food Production: Agricultural Production. Food Production: Animal Source. Food and Beverage Processing. Food and Staples Retailing. Tobacco. Unless exempted by FLAG Criteria Assessment Indicator C1.3. | Indication of main SBTi sector classification in Question R2785 of the portal during Registration. |
| **1.2 Gross FLAG-related emissions magnitude** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies with gross FLAG-related emissions, as detailed in FLAG C3, that equal or exceed 20% of total scope 1, 2 and 3 GHG emissions, in any scope or category in the inventory, must set FLAG targets. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S413, S8A. Provision of the completed commodity and regional breakdowns FLAG Annex, containing the company's FLAG-related emissions magnitudes and data sources in S8A. |
| **1.3 Exemption Case** | Target Setting | Companies within a FLAG-designated sector but with gross FLAG-related emissions <5% of their total GHG emissions may set only energy and industrial (E&I) targets with no FLAG targets, but must include all FLAG-related emissions in the E&I target boundary(ies) in this case. | Portal Location: GHG inventory tab - FLAG. Questions: S411, S413. Confirmation and provision of all the relevant information. |

**FLAG C2 — Target boundaries and emissions coverage:** The FLAG target must cover at least 95% of FLAG-related scope 1 emissions. The FLAG target must cover at least 67% of FLAG-related scope 3 emissions. When included in the FLAG target, FLAG-related scope 3 emissions are separate from a company's energy/industry (non-FLAG) 67% scope 3 target coverage. Each 67% threshold shall be met independently. Companies that meet FLAG criterion 1 (FLAG-C1) and whose scope 3 gross emissions are 40% or more of total scope 1, 2 and 3 emissions, must set a FLAG scope 3 target and an energy/industry scope 3 target. Target coverage must be met separately for FLAG scope 1 and FLAG scope 3 of a company's FLAG GHG inventory.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **2.1 Scope 1 FLAG target boundary** | Target Setting | Companies setting FLAG targets must cover ≥95% of total scope 1 FLAG-related emissions. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target. Questions: S1154. Confirmation of net scope 1 FLAG emissions covered by the scope 1 FLAG target. |
| **2.2 Scope 3 FLAG target requirement** | Target Setting | Companies must set both E&I and FLAG scope 3 targets if they trigger either requirement in FLAG C1.1 or C1.2 and gross scope 3 emissions are 40% or more of total scope 1, 2 and 3 emissions. | Portal Location: Targets tab. Addition of eligible scope 3 energy & industrial and FLAG targets until errors for insufficient scope 3 coverage are no longer triggered. |
| **2.3 Scope 3 FLAG target boundary** | Target Setting | Companies setting scope 3 FLAG targets must cover ≥67% of total gross scope 3 FLAG-related emissions, completely independent of SBTi Near-Term Criterion 6 which considers only E&I target boundaries. | Portal Location: Targets tab. Addition of eligible scope 3 energy & industrial and FLAG targets until errors for insufficient scope 3 coverage are no longer triggered. |
| **2.4 Beyond value chain abatement not included** | Target Setting | Companies must not calculate target coverage including emissions which they intend to reduce which arise outside of the reporting company's value chain, as this would be considered either avoided emissions accounting or consideration of offsets which cannot be considered in FLAG GHG accounting and consequently cannot contribute to target boundaries or corresponding emissions reductions. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S811, S8312. Confirmation that emissions being reported are within the company's value chain. |

**FLAG C3 — Land-related emissions accounting:** Beginning April 2023, companies that meet the relevant criteria are required to account for their land-related emissions and removals from activities occurring within their value chains and include them in a FLAG target.

Land-related emissions accounting must include:

i) LUC emissions: All emissions from LUC, including those associated with livestock feed and conversion of natural forests to plantation forests. Companies shall use either direct LUC (dLUC) or statistical LUC (sLUC) to estimate their LUC emissions across scopes 1 and 3, consistent with the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard.

ii) Land management (non-LUC) emissions: All emissions from land management (biogenic CO2, N2O and CH4). CO2 emissions related to on-farm vehicles and fertilizer production are also included, as they are commonly embedded in accounting tools and emission factors associated with land management.

iii) Carbon removals and storage: Carbon sequestration from improved forest management, agroforestry, forest restoration, silvopasture, soil organic carbon and biochar. Emissions and removals from the production and end use of bioenergy shall not be included in FLAG target setting and shall be addressed in accordance with SBTi general criteria on bioenergy (see criterion C10 and recommendations R3 and R4).

Companies shall calculate their FLAG base year emissions (tCO2e) in line with the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard. Until the effective date of the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard (01/01/2027) companies may use the draft GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Guidance released in 2022.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **3.1 LUC emissions calculation** | GHG Accounting | Companies must use either direct LUC (dLUC) or statistical LUC (sLUC) to estimate their LUC emissions across scopes 1 and 3, consistent with GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard, and covering all types of conversion including those associated with livestock feed and forest conversion to plantation. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A, S821, S823. Confirmation and uploading "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. |
| **3.2 Land management emissions coverage** | GHG Accounting | Companies must calculate and report all land management GHG emissions, covering all relevant GHGs and, if necessary, may even include fossil based emissions such as emissions from on-farm vehicles if included in the emissions factors or lifecycle assessments. Companies may alternatively include on-farm fossil based emissions in energy/industry targets, if they are able to disaggregate those emissions, but must not double count the on-farm fossil based emissions across the FLAG and energy & industrial GHG inventories and target boundaries. Companies reporting on-farm vehicle fossil based emissions within the FLAG inventory must also include these emissions in determining whether specific thresholds, such as FLAG C8, are met. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A, S822, S823, S824. Confirmation and uploading "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. |
| **3.3 FLAG and bioenergy GHG emissions and removals allocation** | GHG Accounting | Companies setting FLAG targets and reporting separate inventories must include all FLAG-related emissions, disaggregated into LUC and land management, and all removals in the FLAG GHG inventory, as detailed in Table 4 in the "Forest, Land and Agriculture Science-Based Target-Setting Guidance V1.2". Companies must not include emissions and removals from bioenergy in the FLAG inventory, rather these must be accounted for in accordance with the SBTi general criteria on bioenergy. | Portal Location: FLAG / GHG inventory tab - General questions. Questions: S8A, S351, S3512, S3515, S3517. Confirmation and uploading "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. |

| **3.4 FLAG emissions alignment with GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard** | Sector-Specific GHG Accounting | Companies may continue using the draft version of the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Guidance to calculate base year and all subsequent reporting years' FLAG-related emissions for submissions up until 31 December 2026. For submissions from 1 January 2027 onwards, the use of the final version of the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard will be required. While the SBTi accepts alignment with either document until 1 January 2027, companies are expected to apply one framework consistently across their inventory rather than selecting reporting requirements from both documents for different activities. In cases where only one of the documents provides methodological guidance for a specific situation relevant to the company, this may be communicated to the validation team. Where justified, a temporary exception may be accepted during the interim period while the SBTi continues to assess the implications of full alignment with the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard by January 2027. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S821, S8211. Confirmation of alignment to either the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard or the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Guidance Draft, along with a declaration of any deviations, if applicable. |
| **3.5 Removals alignment with GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard** | Sector-Specific GHG Accounting | Companies may continue using the draft version of the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Guidance to calculate base year and all subsequent reporting years' FLAG-related removals until 31 December 2026. From 1 January 2027 onwards, the use of the final version of the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard will be required. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S83111, S83114, S8315, S8316. Confirmation. |
| **3.6 All relevant GHGs included** | Target Setting | Companies must calculate and report FLAG-related emissions from all relevant GHGs as per the Kyoto Protocol, unless providing a justified, immaterial exclusion. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A. Confirmation and uploading "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. |
| **3.7 Scope 1 FLAG-related exclusions limit** | Target Setting | Companies must provide clear justification for any exclusions and must not exclude more than 5% of gross scope 1 FLAG-related emissions from the GHG inventory boundary. | Portal Location: FLAG / Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target. Questions: S8A. Confirmation and uploading "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. Demonstration of sufficient target coverage and excluded emissions are taken into account in the total scope 1 emissions when calculating the required coverage. |
| **3.8 Scope 3 FLAG-related exclusions limit** | Target Setting | Companies must provide clear justification for any exclusions and must not exclude more than 5% of gross scope 3 FLAG-related emissions from the GHG inventory boundary. | Portal Location: FLAG / Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target. Questions: S8A, S1154. Confirmation and uploading "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. Demonstration of sufficient target coverage. Use of the formula: (percent of emissions covered by a target within a category) x (percent of emissions that category represents out of total scope 3 emissions) to calculate coverage of total emissions. Excluded emissions are taken into account in the total scope 3 emissions when calculating the required coverage. |

**FLAG C4 — No-deforestation commitment:** Companies shall publicly commit to no-deforestation covering the most important sources of deforestation in their operations. The commitment will be posted on the SBTi target dashboard using the following language: "[Company X] commits to no-deforestation across its primary deforestation-linked commodities, with a target date of [no later than 2 years after FLAG target submission date. The target date cannot be later than 31 December 2030]". The cutoff date is recommended to be no later than 2020. If it is later than 2020, it shall be no later than 3 years prior to submission of the company's first FLAG targets for SBTi validation. Companies are expected to align with a 2020 cutoff date. Where this is not possible for specific portions of their value chain, this shall be disclosed and justified in public documentation regarding their no-deforestation commitment. 2020 or earlier cutoff dates shall be maintained for the other portions of the value chain. Companies shall assess the primary deforestation-linked commodities in their value chains and include them in the commitment. As part of the assessment process, companies shall undertake risk assessment and due diligence processes to understand where primary deforestation-linked commodities exist in their value chains. The assessment shall cover commodities produced, sourced or contained in purchased products as well as commodities embedded as feed for animal products. Primary deforestation-linked commodities to consider in the assessment are defined in Appendix A. Within 12 months of validating its FLAG target, a company shall publish the commitment language on its own website or in relevant self published policy documents. This shall include: The method and outcome of the company's assessment of its primary deforestation-linked commodities. Key information on how the company plans to deliver its no-deforestation commitment either as a standalone document or within relevant documentation. Companies with FLAG no-deforestation commitments validated in line with FLAG-C4 of the SBTi FLAG Guidance V1.0 or V1.1 are recommended to maintain their existing commitment. A company that elects to update its commitment shall: Set an updated target within two years of the company's submission of the updated commitment for SBTi validation, and no later than 31 December 2028. Publicly disclose progress achieved against its previous commitment, including relevant barriers found in the implementation of the commitment, and planned actions to address these barriers prior to revising the commitment. Retain its previous cutoff date if it is aligned with the requirements on cutoff dates in this criterion.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **4.1 Deforestation-linked commodities covered** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Primary deforestation-linked commodities shall include: All commodities directly produced by the company within its scope 1 boundary. All commodities sourced by the company within its scope 3 boundary according to the following thresholds: All globally significant deforestation-linked commodities (cattle, cocoa, coffee, oil palm, rubber, soy, and timber) that represent ≥1% of the company's total sourced FLAG commodity volume in tonnage. All other sourced FLAG commodities that represent ≥5% of the company's total sourced FLAG commodity volume in tonnage, if these commodities pose deforestation risks. Commodities that the company has already assessed as deforestation-free shall be included within the boundary of this commitment to ensure that the no deforestation status is maintained through time. *If a product sourced by the company contains an embedded deforestation-linked commodity in a trivial quantity (less than 1% of the product's total volume in tonnage), the company may exclude this product from the risk assessment described above.* | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S862, S864, S865. List of commodities included in the company's no-deforestation commitment, and evidence for any exclusions based on the significance thresholds. |
| **4.2 Maintaining no deforestation target** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies that have no deforestation-linked commodities or that do have deforestation-linked commodities and believe that no deforestation exists in their operations or supply chains must provide robust justification and evidence for this state. Such companies should commit to no deforestation maintenance targets, taking the form: "[Company Name] commits to maintaining no deforestation across its primary deforestation-linked commodities." | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8631. Provision of evidence demonstrating that the company has no deforestation-linked commodities or has already achieved a state of no deforestation across the operations and/or supply chain. |
| **4.3 No-Deforestation commitment target year** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | The target date for the company's no-deforestation commitment shall be within two years of the company's submission date of FLAG targets for SBTi validation, and no later than 31 December 2030. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S869. Provision of a compliant target date for the No Deforestation commitment. |
| **4.4 New cutoff date requirements** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | The cutoff date is recommended to be no later than 2020. If it is later than 2020, it shall be no later than 3 years prior to submission of the company's first FLAG targets for SBTi validation. Where it is not possible to align with a 2020 or earlier cutoff date for specific portions of the value chain, this shall be disclosed and justified in public documentation regarding the company's no deforestation commitment. 2020 or earlier cutoff dates shall be maintained for the other portions of the value chain. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S866, S867, S868. Provision of the cutoff date, and verification that if the cutoff date is later than 2020, it is not later than 3 years prior to submission of the company's first FLAG targets for SBTi validation. Where it is not possible to align with a 2020 or earlier cutoff date for specific portions of the value chain, confirmation that this will be disclosed and justified in public documentation regarding the company's no deforestation commitment, and confirmation that the 2020 or earlier cutoff date is maintained for the other portions of the value chain. |
| **C4.5 Public Reporting requirements** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Within 12 months of validating their FLAG target, companies shall publish the commitment language either as a standalone document or within relevant documentation. This shall include: The method and outcome of the company's assessment of its primary deforestation-linked commodities. Key information on how they plan to deliver their no-deforestation commitment, on their own website or in relevant self-published policy documents. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8610. Confirmation that the company agrees to publish its no deforestation commitment, as well as the outcome of the risk assessment and its delivery plan within 12 months after the target validation date. |
| **C4.6 No-Deforestation Commitment Target Update conditions** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies with FLAG no-deforestation commitments validated in line with FLAG-C4 of the SBTi FLAG Guidance V1.0 or V1.1 are recommended to maintain their existing commitment. A company that chooses to update its commitment shall: Set an updated no deforestation target with a target date within two years of the company's submission of the updated commitment for SBTi validation, and no later than 31 December 2028. Publicly disclose progress achieved against their previous commitment, including relevant barriers found in the implementation of the commitment, and planned actions to address these barriers prior to revising their commitment. Retain its previous cutoff date if it is aligned with the requirements on cutoff dates in this criterion. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8601, S86011, S86012. Provision of evidence (i.e. external links) where the company has reported progress, barriers, and planned actions to address these barriers prior to updating their target. Confirmation whether the company will retain the same cutoff date as in their latest submission, if it aligns with the cutoff date requirements as outlined in criterion 4. |

**FLAG C5 — FLAG target setting:** Companies must keep FLAG and energy/industry (non-FLAG) targets and accounting separate. FLAG-relevant emissions and removals include those related to agriculture (to farm gate, excluding processing), LUC and land management, including forestry (to yard, excluding processing). For companies with FLAG emissions below the 20% threshold that choose not to set a separate FLAG target, FLAG emissions must be accounted for separately and included in the traditional target. Removals cannot be used in this case. Please note that this FLAG target setting criterion (FLAG-C5) applies for near-term and long-term targets.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **5.1 Separation of GHG inventories** | GHG Accounting | Companies setting FLAG targets must ensure FLAG emissions and E&I emissions are disaggregated into separate GHG inventories. Companies setting FLAG targets must submit two GHG inventories: 1. The energy/industrial GHG emissions inventory. 2. The FLAG GHG emissions inventory. | Portal Location: GHG inventory tab - FLAG. Question: S8A. Provision of FLAG GHG inventory data via CSV upload. |
| **5.2 FLAG and E&I proportions provided** | GHG Accounting | Companies with gross FLAG-related emissions that correspond to less than 20% of total emissions must provide the proportion of FLAG and E&I emissions and details of the determination of FLAG-related emissions to justify no separation of emissions and FLAG target setting. Such companies must provide a breakdown of the FLAG-related emissions and E&I emissions in each scope and category. | Portal Location: GHH inventory tab - FLAG. Questions: S411, S413, S4114. Confirmation. |

**FLAG C6 — Level of ambition:** A FLAG company's target ambition (1.5°C or well below 2°C) will be determined based on the ambition of its energy/industry (non-FLAG) target.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **6.1 Temperature alignment based on E&I targets** | Target Setting | Companies setting FLAG targets must report their temperature alignment according to the target classification determined based on the ambition of its scope 1 and 2 energy/industry (non-FLAG) target. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target. Questions: S111191. Confirmation. |

**FLAG C7 — Use of the agricultural pathways:** Companies may use both the FLAG sector and commodity approaches, with the FLAG sector approach being the most appropriate for companies with diversified land-intensive activities in their supply chain such as companies in midstream and downstream sectors. Supply-side companies may use one of the ten available agricultural commodity pathways only if emissions for that commodity account for 10% or more of a company's total (gross, excluding removals) FLAG emissions (across all scopes). (See also C8 for criterion on use of the timber & wood fiber pathway.)

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **7.1 Disaggregation of FLAG-related emissions by commodity type** | Sector-Specific GHG Accounting | Companies must disaggregate FLAG-related emissions across different products and commodities to enable determination of applicability of different FLAG target setting types. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A. Confirmation and upload "Commodity and regional breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. |
| **7.2 Insufficient commodity specific emissions for commodity pathway** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies with emissions from one of the ten available agricultural commodity pathways that account for less than 10% of a reporting company's total gross FLAG emissions must not use the commodity pathway for that commodity. Above 10%, companies may use the commodity pathway for that commodity. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A. Confirmation and uploading "Commodity and regional breakdown FLAG Annex" CSV files with the required information. |
| **7.3 No absolute emissions increases** | Target Setting | Companies using the commodity- or intensity-based pathways, must not set targets that result in an increase in absolute emissions in the target year relative to emissions in the base year. | Portal Location: Add near-term FLAG target: commodity-specific target. Questions: S11681. Confirmation of completion of the commodity-specific emissions and activity data and clicking calculate ambition. Ambition calculated should prevent absolute emissions increase. |

**FLAG C8 — Use of the timber and wood fiber commodity pathway:** Companies in the forest and paper products sector or with emissions related to timber & wood fiber accounting for 10% or more of their FLAG emissions (gross, excluding removals) are required to use the commodity pathway for timber & wood fiber available in the commodity pathways. Rubber companies must use the sector pathway, not the timber & wood fiber commodity pathway.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **8.1 Application of timber and wood fiber commodity pathway** | Target Setting | Companies with gross FLAG-related emissions corresponding to timber and wood fiber equal to or exceeding 10% of total FLAG-related emissions must cover these emissions with timber and wood fiber commodity pathway targets. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A. Confirmation and uploading "Commodity and regional breakdown FLAG Annex" file with the required information. |

**FLAG C9 — Use of the sub-global pathways for the commodity pathways:** If a commodity pathway is used, sub-global pathways must be applied for the commodity based on commodity sourcing by region/country. In cases where the global pathway is more ambitious than a company's regional pathway, a company may opt to use the global pathway.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **9.1 Regionalized data for sub-global pathway use** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must have adequate regionalised data in order to be eligible to use the commodity pathways. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S8A. Confirmation and uploading "Commodity and regional breakdown FLAG Annex" and "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" files with the required information. |
| **9.2 Sub-global pathway use** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies which are eligible as per FLAG C7 and choosing to set commodity pathway targets must use sub-global commodity pathways, unless the global pathway is more ambitious. | Portal Location: FLAG / Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target.
