Questions: S8A, S1163, S1165, S11657. Confirmation and uploading "Commodity and regional breakdown FLAG Annex" and "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" files with the required information. |

**FLAG C10 — Base and target years:** In alignment with SBTi criteria, targets must cover a minimum of five years and a maximum of ten years from the date the target is submitted to the SBTi for official validation.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **10.1 Target timeframe** | Target Setting | Companies setting FLAG targets must align target timeframe with the SBTi near-term criteria; they must cover a minimum of five years and a maximum of ten years from the date the target is submitted to the SBTi for official validation. If the target is submitted for validation in the first half of the year (i.e., by the end of June), the timeframe includes the year of submission. If submitted in the second half of the year, the timeframe begins from the start of the following year. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target. Questions: S1155, S1164. Confirmation. |
| **10.2 Representative baseline for meaningful target ambition** | Target Setting | Companies setting FLAG targets must ensure the base year chosen corresponds to emissions and activity volumes that are representative of the organizational boundary at the time of submission. Companies should avoid choosing base years where emissions magnitudes and product sourcing are significantly different from those in surrounding years, because of the significant impacts of sourcing on FLAG-related emissions. | Portal Location: GHG inventory - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target. Questions: S741, S11672, S11673. Confirmation and provision of supporting documents displaying recent trajectories in emissions, activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics to justify the choice of base year. |
| **10.3 Consistent reporting period** | Target Setting | Companies setting FLAG targets must use the same reporting period across E&I emissions and FLAG-related emissions for the base year, most recent year, and subsequent reporting years. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Reporting years / Targets tab - Add near-term FLAG target / Targets tab - Add long-term FLAG target. Questions: S212, S216, S1155. Confirmation and displaying the base year and target year entered for all the energy and industrial and FLAG targets in the Targets section of the Validation Portal. |
| **10.4 Consistent base year** | Target Setting | Companies setting FLAG targets must use the same base year for FLAG targets and E&I targets over each scope. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Reporting years. Questions: S212, S216. Confirmation and displaying the base year and target year entered for all the E&I and FLAG targets in the Targets section of the Validation Portal. |

**FLAG C11 — Target validation and reporting:** Companies must report removals and emissions separately for both baseline and annual emissions accounting. Companies are expected to deliver both emission reductions and carbon dioxide removals in line with the 1.5°C pathways. Removing carbon from the atmosphere as a result of land-management activities should not be used to reduce the level of emission reductions within the FLAG target boundary, and companies should mostly focus on emission reductions. (Note that emission reductions represent 62% of the mitigation potential in the FLAG Sector Pathway.)

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **11.1 Separate removals and reductions reporting** | Sector-Specific GHG Accounting | Companies set FLAG targets over net FLAG-related emissions (land-related emissions combined with removals) in the validation process, but companies must report emissions, reductions and removals accounting separately if removals accounting meets the necessary GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard quality criteria. For companies who submit data that has removals netted within the figures, or submits data with no removals, robust justification should be provided, as well as plans to rectify the data limitation in future iterations of their FLAG targets following the requirements of the GHG Protocol Land Sector and Removals Standard. | Portal Location: FLAG. Questions: S83114, S8315, S8316. Confirmation and uploading "Commodity and regional breakdown FLAG Annex" and "Emissions source breakdown FLAG Annex" files with the required information. |

**FLAG C12 — Target aggregation:** When aggregating FLAG targets across commodities and/or approaches, companies must report on sub-targets, in addition to the overarching, aggregated target, in their validation form. Companies shall achieve the aggregated target, and they shall also achieve their sub-targets (e.g., scope 1, scope 3, individual commodities).

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **12.1 Target progress reporting** | Sector-Specific Measurement, Reporting and Verification | Companies reporting on progress against FLAG targets that are aggregated across commodities and/or approaches must report on sub-targets, in addition to the overarching, aggregated target, in their validation form. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add combined targets / Progress and reporting. Questions: S1013211, S1013221 / S1211, S1212, S1213. Confirmation whether aggregated targets will be communicated with sub-targets included in the target language and corresponding confirmation of commitment to report progress against overarching target and sub-targets on an annual basis. |

## MARITIME SECTOR

### Table 10. Maritime Shipping Sector Criteria Assessment Table

**Shipping C1 — Target Year eligibility:** For all companies using this guidance, the choice of near-term target year must be no earlier than 2030.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **1.1 Appropriate near-term target year** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport SDA targets, regardless of whether covering own or subcontracted operations, must not set a near-term target year earlier than 2030. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: SMA11210. Confirmation and upload 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' in the Targets section for the relevant target in the Validation Portal. |

**Shipping C2 — Target Requirement:** All companies setting near-term science-based targets covering emissions from own operations (e.g. vessel owners or operators) shall also submit long-term science-based targets along with their near-term target submission. For maritime transport emissions, a long-term science-based target means reducing emissions to a residual level in line with 1.5°C scenarios by no later than 2040. Companies using this guidance to set near-term science-based targets covering scope 3 emissions from subcontracted maritime transport operations (e.g. cargo owners or shippers) are not required to submit long-term science-based targets.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **2.1 Long-Term maritime transport target requirement** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting near-term maritime transport SDA targets covering emissions from own operations (e.g. vessel owners or operators) must also submit Long-Term maritime transport SDA targets with their near-term target submission. For maritime transport emissions, a long-term science-based target means reducing emissions to a residual level in line with 1.5°C scenarios by no later than 2040. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add long-term sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: SMA11411, SMA11143, SMA11145, SMA11146, SMA11148, SMA11410, SMA11411, SMA11413, SMA11414, SMA11420, SMA11424. Provision of required information with supporting documents where applicable and upload 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' in the Targets section for the relevant target in the Validation Portal. |

**Shipping C3 — Optional or Mandatory Maritime Transport SDA Targets:** The maritime transport sector guidance "SCIENCE BASED TARGET SETTING FOR THE MARITIME TRANSPORT SECTOR" and associated maritime transport sector SDA targets are applicable to and optional for companies that derive 5% or more of their scope 1 and 2 GHG emissions (tCO2e) from maritime transportation activities, corresponding to emissions from any vessel type listed in Appendix 2 of the guidance. Long-term maritime transport SDA targets are mandatory when near-term maritime transport SDA targets have been set over maritime transport activities within their organizational boundary.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **3.1 Appropriate activities for maritime transport sector scope 1 and scope 3 category 3 SDA targets** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must have maritime transport TTW emissions within their organizational boundary, corresponding to scope 1 emissions that equal or exceed 5% of total scope 1 and 2 emissions, in order to be eligible to set scope 1 and scope 3 category 3 maritime transport SDA targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview. Questions: S52, S731. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 business activities and breakdown of key scope 1 emissions. |

**Shipping C4 — WTW Emissions Coverage of Each Vessel Type:** Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets must cover complete WTW maritime transport emissions in the respective target boundaries, disaggregating overall maritime transport emissions and activity into each relevant vessel type for target calculation and aggregating subsequently.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **4.1 WTW target boundary** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport SDA targets must cover all WTW emissions corresponding to the selected vessel type in the maritime transport SDA target boundary, regardless of whether WTW emissions are reported across scopes (TTW emissions in scope 1 and WTT emissions in scope 3) or entirely WTW within scope 3. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory - Scope 3 - Fuel and energy related activities / GHG Inventory - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: S52, S6313, S731, SMA1125 for near-term target / SMA1145 for long-term target. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 business activities and breakdown of key scope 1 emissions and and scope 3 GHG emissions, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the target boundary. |
| **4.2 Additional scope 1 and 2 targets covering significant non-maritime transport sector emissions** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must set eligible cross-sector or alternative relevant sector-specific targets over scope 1 and 2 emissions not covered by maritime transport sector SDA targets if maritime transport TTW emissions constitute between 5% and 95% of total scope 1 and 2 emissions and are covered by maritime transport sector SDA targets to ensure total scope 1 and 2 coverage is at least 95%. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term target / Targets tab - Add long-term target. Questions: S52, S522, S731. Confirmation of business activities and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the target boundary of the relevant targets. |
| **4.2 Additional scope 3 targets covering significant non-maritime transport sector emissions** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must set eligible cross-sector or alternative relevant sector-specific targets over scope 3 emissions not covered by maritime transport sector SDA targets if maritime transport emissions constitute less than 67% of total scope 3 emissions, and are covered by maritime transport sector SDA targets, to ensure total scope 3 coverage is at least 67%. This is subject to Near-Term Criterion 4. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term target. Questions: S61, S731. Confirmation and description of key scope 3 business activities in Questions alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the target setting tools and target boundary in the Targets section of the validation portal. |
| **4.4 Insignificant maritime transport sector emissions and SDA applicability** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must set eligible cross-sector absolute reduction targets or SDA targets rather than maritime transport SDA targets if maritime transport TTW emissions constitute <5% of total scope 1 and 2 GHG emissions. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term target / Targets tab - Add long-term target. Questions: S52, S522, S731. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the target boundary of the relevant targets. |
| **4.5 Scope 3 maritime transport sector emissions and SDA target coverage** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets over outsourced/subcontracted maritime transport activities must report and target the scope 3 emissions on a WTW basis in their respective activity's category. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory - Scope 3 - Fuel and energy related activities / GHG Inventory - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: S6413, S731, SMA1125 for near-term target / SMA1145 for long-term target. Confirmation and breakdown of key scope 3 GHG emissions, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the target boundary. |
| **4.6 Disaggregation of emissions and activity into vessel type target boundaries** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport SDA targets, irrespective of ownership, must model targets for respective vessel types, specific vessel size buckets, and their specific WTW emissions and metric gigatonne-nautical miles or metric tonne-nautical miles transported. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: S731 / SMA1123, SMA1125 for near-term target / SMA1143, SMA1145 for long-term target. Confirmation, provision of required information with supporting documents where applicable and uploading 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' in the Targets section of the Validation Portal for both near-term and long-term targets. |
| **4.7 Aggregation of sub-targets for official target language** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport SDA targets may aggregate all sub-targets over different vessel types to result in target language which must follow the following format. Own operations: "[Company Name] commits to reduce well-to-wake scope 1 and 3 GHG emissions from [vessel type*] shipping operations % by [target year] from a [base year] base year." Subcontracted operations: "[Company Name] commits to reduce reduce well-to-wake scope 3 GHG emissions from subcontracted [vessel type*] shipping operations % by [target year] from a [base year] base year." *where subcontracted and vessel type is only specified for targets covering only a specific type, such as 'container'. | Portal Location: Submissions elements - Targets tab / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: 10.13.1.1, 10.13.2.1 for near-term target / 10.13.2.2 for long-term target. Confirmation, provision of required information with supporting documents where applicable and upload 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' in the Targets section of the Validation Portal for both near-term and long-term targets. |

**Shipping C5 — Base Year Suitability:** Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets must ensure the selected base year is representative of current business activities and consistent across scope 1, 2 and scope 3.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **5.1 Representative baseline for meaningful target ambition** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets must ensure the base year chosen corresponds to emissions and activity volumes that are representative of the organizational boundary at the time of submission. Companies should avoid choosing base years where emissions magnitudes and activity (metric gigaton-nautical miles for passenger operations or metric tonne-nautical miles for freight operations) are significantly different from those in surrounding years, because of the significant impacts of activity levels on resulting target ambition. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: S731 / SMA1123, SMA1125 for near-term target / SMA1143, SMA1145 for long-term target. |
| **5.2 Appropriate base year** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport SDA targets, regardless of whether covering own or subcontracted operations, must not set a base year earlier than 2018. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory - Reporting years / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: S216 / SMA11220 for near term target / SMA11420 for long-term target. Provision of required information with supporting documents where applicable and uploading 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' for in the Targets section of the Validation Portal for both near-term and long-term targets. |

**Shipping C6 — Activity Disclosure and Projections:** Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets must disclose and report base year, most recent year and target year activity data, in terms of metric gigaton-nautical miles or metric tonne-nautical miles transported depending on the vessel type, with credible and justifiable growth projections to determine minimum target ambition which must be aligned with or exceed their 1.5°C pathway convergence curve's minimum ambition for scope 1 and scope 3 category 3 targets and which must be aligned with or exceed their WB2C pathway convergence curve's minimum ambition for solely scope 3 targets.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **6.1 Disclosure of current organization maritime transport activity** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets must disclose base year and most recent year metric gigaton-nautical miles (passenger operations) or metric tonne-nautical miles (freight operations) transported corresponding to scope 1 and 2 emissions. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: SMA1126, SMA1128 for near-term target / SMA1146, SMA1148 for long-term target. Confirmation and uploading the associated 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' for both near-term and long-term targets. |
| **6.2 Disclosure of credible and justifiable activity projections over organization's maritime transport** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year metric gigaton-nautical miles or metric tonne-nautical miles transported corresponding to scope 1 and 2 emissions. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: SMA112111, SMA11213 for near-term target / SMA114111, SMA11413 for long-term target. Confirmation and provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories in activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics result in the growth projections included in the target setting tool. |
| **6.3 Disclosure of current value chain maritime transport activity** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets over WTW maritime transport emissions where TTW are also reported in scope 3 must disclose corresponding base year and most recent year metric gigaton-nautical miles or metric tonne-nautical miles transported. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: SMA1126, SMA1128 for near-term target / SMA1146, SMA1148 for long-term target. Confirmation and uploading the associated 'SBT Maritime Transport Tool' for both near-term and long-term targets. |
| **6.4 Disclosure of credible and justifiable activity projections over value chain maritime transport** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting maritime transport sector SDA targets over maritime transport TTW emissions reported in scope 3 must disclose credible and justifiable corresponding projected target year metric gigaton-nautical miles or metric tonne-nautical miles transported. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Maritime SDA. Questions: SMA112111, SMA11213 for near-term target / SMA114111, SMA11413 for long-term target. Confirmation and provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories in activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics result in the growth projections included in the target setting tool. |

## POWER SECTOR

### Table 11. Power Sector Criteria Assessment Table

**Power C1 — Applicability of Power SDA targets:** The power sector guidance "SETTING 1.5°C-ALIGNED SCIENCE-BASED TARGETS: QUICK START GUIDE FOR ELECTRIC UTILITIES" and associated power sector SDA targets are applicable to and mandatory for companies that derive 5% or more of their scope 1 and 2 GHG emissions (tCO2e) from electricity generation activities which are not wholly from renewable sources.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **1.1 Appropriate activities for self-generation power SDA targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies must have electricity generation emissions within their organizational boundary, corresponding to scope 1 emissions that are 5% or more of total scope 1 and 2 emissions, in order to be eligible to set scope 1 and scope 3 category 3 maritime transport SDA targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation. Questions: S52, S522, SPG1125 for near-term target, SPG1145 for long-term target. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **1.2 Mandatory scope 1 power SDA targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies with electricity generation emissions within their organizational boundary corresponding to ≥5% of total scope 1 and 2 emissions must set a scope 1 power SDA target. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation. Questions: S52, S522, SPG1125 for near-term target / SPG1145 for long-term target. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **1.3 Mandatory all sold electricity power SDA targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies that buy and resell electricity alongside generation activities in their organizational boundary must also set an all sold electricity power SDA target. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Fuel and energy-related activities / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: S52, S522, S6313, S1125 for near-term target / S1145 for long-term target. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities as well as confirmation and breakdown of key scope 3 GHG emissions in category 3, corresponding to purchased and resold electricity, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **1.4 Inappropriate activities for self-generation power SDA targets** | Target Setting | Companies that generate electricity from 100% renewable sources must model their scope 1 and 2 targets using the absolute reduction method. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - General questions / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2. Questions: S312, S52, S522, S11114 for near-term target / S11314 for long-term target. Confirmation of business activities and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **1.5 Appropriate activities for only all-sold electricity power SDA targets** | Target Setting | Companies that only purchase and resell electricity - or that generate electricity from 100% renewable sources but also purchase and resell electricity - with associated generation emissions exceeding 5% of total scope 3, must still set an all-sold electricity power SDA target. Such companies with 100% renewable self-generation should avoid inclusion of the self-generation emissions and MWh activity in the determination of emissions intensity. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - General questions / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Fuel and energy-related activities / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: S312, S52, S522, S6313, S731 / S1125 for near-term target / S1145 for long-term target. Confirmation of business activities in Question S312, description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities in Questions S52 and S522 in the GHG inventory section of the Validation Portal, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the Targets section of the Validation Portal. |

**Power C2 — All-Sold Electricity Emissions Targeted:** Companies setting power sector SDA targets must cover emissions from the generation of all sold electricity through a scope 1 target covering self-generated electricity alongside a scope 1 and scope 3 category 3 target covering self-generation and purchased and resold electricity's generation emissions.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **2.1 Expanded target boundary covering insignificant non-power sector emissions** | Target Setting | Companies setting power sector SDA targets with ≥95% of total scope 1 and 2 emissions from electricity generation may include the remaining scope 1 and 2 GHG emissions in the self-generation and all-sold electricity power SDA target boundaries, but must cover all electricity generation emissions in this case. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: S52, S522, S731 / SPG1125, SPG1145 for near-term and long-term Power SDA: Own Generation target / S1125, S1145 for near-term and long-term Power SDA: All sold electricity target. Confirmation of business activities and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **2.2 Expanded target boundary covering heat** | Target Setting | Companies may include emissions from heat generated and sold as well as emissions from purchased electricity for own use within both the self-generation and all-sold electricity power SDA target boundaries, but must cover all electricity generation emissions in this case. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: S52, S522, S731 / SPG1125, SPG1145 for near-term and long-term Power SDA: Own Generation target / S1125, S1145 for near-term and long-term Power SDA: All sold electricity target. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **2.3 Additional targets covering significant non-power sector emissions** | Target Setting | Companies must set ACA or other relevant SDA targets over scope 1 and 2 emissions not covered by power sector SDA targets if electricity generation emissions constitute between 5% and 95% of total scope 1 and 2 emissions and are covered power sector SDA targets to ensure total scope 1 and 2 coverage is at least 95%. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term target / Targets tab - Add long-term target. Questions: S52, S522, S731. Confirmation of business activities and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **2.4 Insignificant power sector emissions and SDA applicability** | Target Setting | Companies must not set power sector SDA targets if electricity generation emissions constitute <5% of total scope 1 and 2 GHG emissions. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2. Questions: S52, S522. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities. |

| **2.5 Upstream scope 3 power sector emissions** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting power sector SDA targets must cover purchased and resold electricity's upstream generation emissions with an all-sold electricity power SDA target. This supersedes Near-Term Criterion 4, 6 and 18. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Fuel and energy-related activities / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: S6313, S1125 for near-term target / S1145 for long-term target. Confirmation and breakdown of key scope 3 GHG emissions in category 3, corresponding to purchased and resold electricity, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |

**Power C3 — Suitable Baseline For Meaningful Targets:** Companies setting power sector SDA targets must ensure that the selected base year is representative of current business activities and consistent across scope 1, 2 and 3.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **3.1 Representative baseline for meaningful target ambition** | Target Setting | Companies setting power sector SDA targets should avoid base years where emissions magnitudes and total MWh are significantly different from surrounding years, as this could lead to unambitious or inappropriately ambitious targets. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: SPG1126, SPG1128 for near-term own generation / SPG1146, SPG1148 for long-term own generation / S1126, S1128 for near-term all sold / S1146, S1148 for long-term all sold. Confirmation that base year emissions and activity data are representative of current business activities. |

**Power C4 — Disclosing Activity Projections To Set Ambitious Targets:** Companies setting power sector SDA targets must disclose and report base year, most recent year and target year self-generated and purchased and resold electricity activity data and justification of growth projections to determine minimum target ambition.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **4.1 Disclosure of current organization activity** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting power sector SDA targets must disclose base year and most recent year MWh of electricity generated corresponding to scope 1 and 2 emissions. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: SPG1126, SPG1128 for near-term own generation / SPG1146, SPG1148 for long-term own generation / S1126, S1128 for near-term all sold / S1146, S1148 for long-term all sold. Confirmation and uploading the associated target setting tool for both near-term and long-term targets. |
| **4.2 Disclosure of credible and justifiable organization activity projections** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting power sector SDA targets must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year MWh of electricity generated corresponding to scope 1 and 2 emissions. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: SPG11211, SPG11213, SPG11214 for near-term own generation / S11211, S11213, S11214 for near-term all sold. Confirmation and provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories result in the growth projections. |
| **4.3 Disclosure of current upstream power sector activity** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting power sector SDA targets must disclose electricity generation emissions in scope 3 category 3 corresponding to purchased and resold electricity, and base year and most recent year MWh of electricity purchased and resold. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: SPG1126, SPG1128 for near-term own generation / S1126, S1128 for near-term all sold. Confirmation and uploading the associated target setting tool for both near-term and long-term targets. |
| **4.4 Disclosure of credible and justifiable upstream activity projections** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies setting power sector SDA targets must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year MWh of electricity purchased and resold. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: SPG11211, SPG11213, SPG11214 for near-term own generation / S11211, S11213, S11214 for near-term all sold. Confirmation and provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories result in the growth projections. |
| **4.5 Target year** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Power sector SDA long-term targets must have a target year no later than 2040. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: Own Generation / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Power SDA: All sold electricity. Questions: SPG11410 for own generation / S.11.2.10 for all sold. Confirmation that target year is no later than 2040 for long-term power targets. |

**Power C5 — Distributed And/Or Sold Fossil Fuels:** Companies setting power SDA targets frequently also own assets involved in distribution, transmission or sale of fossil fuel products. Emissions from the combustion of any such distributed, transmitted or sold fossil fuels must be reported in scope 3 category 11. Companies must set cross-sector absolute reduction targets over 100% of these emissions consistent with the level of decarbonization required to keep global temperature increase to 1.5°C, irrespective of the share of these emissions.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **5.1 Inclusion of fossil fuel emissions** | Target Setting | Emissions from the combustion of fossil fuels distributed or transmitted must be accounted for in the GHG inventory and target boundary, even if not sold directly by the reporting company. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products. Questions: S61113, S11114 for near-term cross-sector / S11314 for long-term cross-sector. Confirmation that emissions from combustion of fossil fuels distributed or transmitted are included in GHG inventory. |
| **5.2 Target coverage of fossil fuel emissions** | Target Setting | Companies must disclose if relevant and submit a scope 3 target covering 100% of downstream fossil fuels. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term target / Targets tab - Add long-term target. Questions: S61113, S11114, S11119 for near-term / S11314, S11319 for long-term. Confirmation that scope 3 target covers 100% of downstream fossil fuel emissions. |
| **5.3 Assessment of ambition over fossil fuel emissions** | Target Setting | The ambition of the target covering downstream fossil fuel emissions must be at a minimum aligned with the 1.5°C ambition threshold. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term target / Targets tab - Add long-term target. Questions: S11119 for near-term / S11319 for long-term. Confirmation that target ambition is aligned with the 1.5°C ambition threshold. |

## STEEL SECTOR

### Table 12. Steel Sector Criteria Assessment Table

**Steel C1 — Use of system boundary:** Where the iron & steel SDA is used, emissions covered shall align with the iron & steel core boundary as defined in this document. The intensity denominator is hot rolled steel. Steelmakers using the absolute contraction method shall include all activities within the boundary.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **1.1 Iron & steel core boundary target coverage** | Sector-Specific | Companies must cover ≥95% of all iron & steel core boundary activity emissions in the target boundary, regardless of whether activities occur within the organizational boundary, upstream or downstream in the value chain. This applies to both near-term and long-term steel SDA targets and eligible long-term cross-sector targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Purchased goods and services / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Processing of sold products / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products. Questions: S52, S522, S6113, S61013, S61113, S731 / SST1125 for near-term / SST1145 for long-term. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities as well as key scope 3 GHG emissions inside and outside the iron & steel core boundary, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **1.2 Hot rolled steel activity reporting** | Sector-Specific | Companies must use metric tonnes of hot rolled steel as the denominator in determining emissions intensity for target setting. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: SST1125, SST1126, SST128 for near-term target / SST1145, SST1146, SST148 for long-term target. Confirmation that metric tonnes of hot rolled steel is used as the denominator and uploading the associated target setting tool. |

**Steel C2 — Limitations in use of iron & steel SDA:** The iron & steel SDA may be used for target-setting covering emissions included in the iron & steel core boundary where the final product is steel. If scope 1 and 2 emissions from the iron & steel core boundary constitute less than 95% of total scope 1 and 2 emissions, the remainder must be covered by a different target. If scope 1 and 2 emissions from the core boundary constitute ≥95% of total scope 1 and 2, the company may include those emissions within the core boundary target.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **2.1 Additional targets covering significant non-steel sector emissions** | Target Setting | If iron & steel core boundary activity emissions constitute between 5% and 95% of total scope 1 and 2, companies must set eligible cross-sector absolute reduction or SDA targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / GHG Inventory tab - Overview. Questions: S52, S522, S731. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |
| **2.2 Insignificant steel sector emissions and SDA applicability** | Target Setting | Companies must set eligible cross-sector absolute reduction targets or SDA targets rather than iron & steel SDA targets if iron & steel core boundary activity scope 1 and 2 emissions constitute less than 5% of total scope 1 and 2 GHG emissions. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 1 / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 2 / Targets tab - Add near-term target. Questions: S6113, S731. Confirmation and description of key scope 1 and 2 business activities, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |

**Steel C3 — Near-term scope 3 coverage: purchased intermediate products:** Company science-based targets shall include suppliers' upstream emissions for purchased intermediate products falling within the iron & steel core boundary, irrespective of whether the share is ≥40%, and irrespective of scope 3 coverage by other targets.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **3.1 Upstream scope 3 steel sector emissions and SDA target coverage** | Sector-Specific | Companies must cover iron & steel core boundary activity emissions in scope 3 category 1, related to purchased intermediate products, in the overall iron & steel SDA target. Total coverage must equal or exceed 95%. This supersedes Near-Term Criterion 4, 6 and 18. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Purchased goods and services / Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: S52, S522, S73 / SST1125 for near-term / SST1145 for long-term. Confirmation and breakdown of key scope 3 GHG emissions in category 1, related to purchased intermediate products, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |

**Steel C4 — Near-term scope 3 coverage: sold intermediate products:** Science-based targets shall include downstream emissions associated with further processing of sold intermediate products falling within the iron & steel core boundary, irrespective of whether the share is ≥40% and irrespective of scope 3 coverage.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **4.1 Downstream scope 3 steel sector emissions and SDA target coverage** | Sector-Specific | Companies must cover iron & steel core boundary activity emissions in scope 3 category 10 related to sold intermediate products AND scope 3 category 11 related to use of sold off-gases from steel production activities, in the overall iron & steel SDA target. Total coverage must equal or exceed 95%. This supersedes Near-Term Criteria 4, 6 and 18. This does NOT supersede Near-Term Criterion 22 — emissions related to sold coke or other fossil fuels must be covered in totality targets with ambition equalling or exceeding an appropriate 1.5°C pathway. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Processing of sold products / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products. Questions: S61013, S61113, S731 / SST1125 for near-term / SST1145 for long-term. Confirmation and breakdown of key scope 3 GHG emissions related to sold intermediate products, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes. |

**Steel C5 — Near-term scope 3 target covering category 3: upstream fuel- and energy-related emissions:** Near-term iron & steelmakers science-based targets shall include a scope 3 target that covers all scope 3 category 3 "fuel- and energy-related emissions not included in scope 1 or scope 2" according to the GHG Protocol.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **5.1 Mandatory scope 3 category 3: fuel- and energy-related activities emissions targeting** | Sector-Specific | Companies considered 'steelmakers' or 'ironmakers' by the definitions on page 9 of the guidance document must include a scope 3 target that covers all scope 3 category 3 fuel- and energy-related activities emissions. These emissions are outside of the iron & steel core boundary and so should not be included in the steel SDA target. This supersedes SBTi Near-Term Criterion 4, 6 and 18. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Fuel and energy-related activities. Questions: S6313, SST11223. Confirmation and breakdown of key GHG emission sources in scope 3 category 3: fuel- and energy-related activities emissions, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes covered under the relevant target. |

**Steel C6 — Forecast growth:** Where the iron & steel SDA is used for target-setting, the company shall provide justification of the growth projection used to calculate the target, including public or internal documents where growth projections are mentioned if relevant.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **6.1 Representative baseline for meaningful target ambition** | Target Setting | Base year must correspond to emissions and activity volumes representative of the organizational boundary at the time of submission. Companies should avoid base years where emissions magnitudes and metric tonnes of hot rolled steel are significantly different from surrounding years. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: S741. Confirmation that base year emissions and activity data are representative of current business activities. |
| **6.2 Disclosure of current activity** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must disclose base year and most recent year metric tonnes of hot rolled steel produced in total, summing that produced internally and in the value chain, as well as the scrap ratio. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: SST1126, SST1127, SST1128, SST1129 for near-term / SST1146, SST1147, SST1148, SST1149 for long-term. Confirmation in the Validation Portal and uploading the associated target setting tool. |
| **6.3 Disclosure of credible and justifiable activity projections** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year metric tonnes of hot rolled steel produced and scrap ratio corresponding to iron & steel core boundary emissions in the GHG inventory. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: SST11210, SST11211, SST11213, SST11214. Provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories result in the growth projections. |

**Steel C7 — Target Wording:** Where the iron & steel SDA is used by iron- or steelmakers for target-setting, the fact that the target calculation depends on scrap share shall be included in the target wording.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **7.1 Scrap ratio impacts stated in target language** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting iron & steel SDA targets must publicly disclose that the target calculation depends on the scrap ratio in the target wording, including in future target reporting. The wording must take the form: "As this target calculation depends on the scrap ratio projection, [Company name] will publish the scrap ratio associated with this target annually starting from the base year." | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: SST11222, SST11224. Confirmation that the required scrap ratio wording is included in the target language. |

**Steel C8 — Annual emissions and scrap input reporting:** Where the iron & steel SDA is used by iron- or steelmakers for target-setting, annual disclosure of both emissions and scrap ratio aligned with the boundary of the target is mandatory.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **8.1 Public annual scrap ratio reporting** | Sector-Specific | Companies must commit to publicly disclose the scrap ratio in the base year and all subsequent reporting years. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: S1212. Confirmation of commitment to annual public disclosure of scrap ratio. |
| **8.2 Public annual target boundary emissions reporting** | Sector-Specific | Companies must commit to publicly disclose iron & steel core boundary emissions in the target boundary corresponding to metric tonnes of hot rolled steel produced. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add sector-specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: S1212. Confirmation of commitment to annual public disclosure of iron & steel core boundary emissions. |



**Steel C8 CAI 8.2 documentation (cont.):** Confirmation in the Validation Portal that annual reports including GHG inventory and progress towards published targets will be published annually.

**Steel C9 — Justification in the case of decreasing scrap ratio:** Iron- or steelmakers planning a reduction in their scrap ratio included in their target shall submit justification of this scrap ratio reduction when submitting their target for validation, and disclose the fact that the calculation was based on a decreasing scrap ratio in public documents.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **9.1 Justification of decreasing scrap ratio** | Sector-Specific Target Setting | Companies must disclose the projected target year scrap ratio to the SBTi and where the scrap ratio is projected to decrease across the target timeframe, companies must justify such projections and plans. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Steel SDA / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Steel SDA. Questions: SST11210, SST11211, SST11213 and SST11214. Provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories in activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics result in the scrap ratio projections included for setting the targets. |
| **9.2 Public disclosure of decreasing scrap ratio and target impacts** | Sector-Specific Measurement, reporting and verification | Companies considered 'ironmakers' and/or 'steelmakers' as defined on page 9 of the guidance "Steel Science-Based Target-Setting Guidance v1.0" planning a reduction in their scrap ratio, included in their target, must publicly disclose the fact that the ambition calculation was based on a decreasing scrap ratio. | Portal Location: Progress and reporting. Questions: S1211, S1212, S1213. Confirmation in the Validation Portal that annual reports including GHG inventory and progress towards published targets will be published annually. |
