## TRANSPORT SECTOR

### Table 13. Transport Sector: Land Transport Criteria Assessment Table

**Land Transport C1 — Well-to-Wheel (WTW) Emissions Coverage of Each Transport Category:** All targets (absolute or intensity) covering land transport activities must be on a WTW basis. Refer to the GLEC Framework V3.0 on how Tank-to-Wheel (TTW) and WTT are accounted for across scopes and categories.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **1.1 Scope 3 transport sector emissions and target coverage** | Target Setting | Companies setting transport sector SDA targets over scope 3 transport activities must report and target the transport activity emissions on a WTW basis within each respective scope 3 category. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Land Transport SDA. Questions: S731, SLT1125. Confirmation and provision of all the required information as required in the Targets section of the Validation Portal. |

**Land Transport C2 — Activity Disclosure and Projections:** Companies setting transport sector SDA targets must disclose and report base year, most recent year and target year activity data, in terms of passenger-kilometers or metric tonne-kilometers transported depending on the transport category, with credible and justifiable growth projections.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **2.1 Disclosure of current value chain land transport activity** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting transport sector SDA targets over transport WTW emissions reported in scope 3 must disclose corresponding base year and most recent year passenger-kilometers or metric tonne-kilometers purchased. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Land Transport SDA. Questions: SLT1126, SLT1128. Provision of all the required information as required in the Targets section of the Validation Portal. |
| **2.2 Representative baseline for meaningful target ambition** | Target Setting | Companies setting transport sector SDA targets must ensure the base year chosen corresponds to emissions and activity volumes that are representative of the organization's normal activities at the time of submission. Companies should avoid choosing base years where emissions magnitudes and passenger-kilometers or metric tonne-kilometers are significantly different from those in surrounding years, because of the significant impacts of activity levels on resulting target ambition. Companies should return to the SBTi to recalculate targets if the targets are later determined to be calculated based on an unrepresentative or unsuitable base year. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Overview. Questions: S741. Provision of supporting documents displaying recent trajectories in emissions, activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics to justify the choice of base year. |
| **2.3 Disclosure of credible and justifiable activity projections** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting transport sector SDA targets over land transport WTW emissions must disclose credible and justifiable corresponding projected target year activity in terms of passenger-kilometers or metric tonne-kilometers. The projected activity for each transport category must correspond to the expected target year activity of that specific transport category. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Land Transport SDA. Questions: SLT11211, SLT11213, SLT11214. Provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories in activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics result in the growth projections considered for setting the target. |

**Land Transport C3 — Emissions Allocation Eligibility:** For all companies using the SDA Transport Tool to set transport SDA targets, the emissions covered must be in scope 3, related to transportation activities outside of the company's organizational boundary.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **3.1 Appropriate activities and emissions allocation** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting transport SDA targets must only cover scope 3 GHG emissions from relevant transportation activities as the most ambitious currently available pathway is insufficiently ambitious for scope 1 and 2 emissions target setting. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Land Transport SDA. Questions: S731, SLT1125, SLT11213, SLT11214. Provision of all the required information as required in the GHG inventory and Targets sections of the Validation Portal. |
| **3.2 Appropriate activities for transport sector scope 3 SDA targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies must have WTW emissions reported in any of categories 4, 6, 7 or 9 from 2-3 Wheelers, Light duty vehicles, Buses, Mini-buses, Medium freight trucks, Heavy freight trucks, Urban rail, Non-urban rail or Rail transport activities to be eligible to set optional transport sector SDA targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Upstream transportation and distribution / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Business travel / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Employee commuting / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Downstream transportation and distribution / GHG Inventory tab - Overview. Questions: S6413, S6613, S613, S6913, S731. Provision of all the required information as required in the GHG inventory section of the Validation Portal. |

**Land Transport C4 — Optional or Mandatory Transport SDA Targets:** The transport sector guidance "Transport Science-Based Target-Setting Guidance (2018)" and associated transport sector well-below 2°C SDA targets are applicable to and optional for companies with scope 3 GHG emissions (tCO2e) from passenger and/or freight transportation activities, as listed in the 'type of transport-related emissions' column in Table 1 of that 2018 transport sector guidance. (The transport SDA shall not be used by automakers to set targets covering scope 3 category 11.)

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **4.1 Appropriate activities for transport sector scope 3 SDA targets** | Target Setting | Companies must have WTW emissions reported in any of categories 4, 6, 7 or 9 from 2-3 Wheelers, Light duty vehicles, Buses, Mini-buses, Medium freight trucks, Heavy freight trucks, Urban rail, Non-urban rail or Rail activities to be eligible to set optional transport sector SDA targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Upstream transportation and distribution / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Business travel / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Employee commuting / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Downstream transportation and distribution / GHG Inventory tab - Overview. Questions: S6413, S6613, S613, S6913, S731. Provision of all the required information as required in the GHG inventory section of the Validation Portal. |

**Land Transport C5 — Disclosure of Sub-targets:** Where intensity targets set for scope 3 using the transport SDA are aggregated with other scope 3 targets on an absolute basis, the intensity sub-target shall also be disclosed in target wording and in annual reporting.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **5.1 Transport category specific targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting transport sector SDA targets over scope 3 transport WTW emissions from more than one transport category option in the target setting tool (e.g. heavy freight trucks and rail transport) must determine minimum ambition requirements for each respective transport category with specific SDA targets. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add combined target / Progress and reporting. Questions: S1013211, S1013221 / S1211, SS1212, S1213. Confirmation whether aggregated targets will be communicated with sub-targets included in the target language and corresponding confirmation of commitment to report progress against overarching target and sub-targets on an annual basis. |
| **5.2 Disclosure of all sub-targets if aggregating** | Sector-Specific | Companies modeling any number of transport sector SDA targets over multiple transport categories in their value chain may aggregate the targets, including with other scope 3 targets, into an aggregated scope 3 target in the target language, but must still disclose each category specific SDA target in the target language and annual reporting, even if considered sub-targets of an overall aggregated transport target. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add combined target. Questions: S1013211, S1013221. Confirmation whether aggregated targets will be communicated with sub-targets included in the target language. |

---

### Table 14. Transport Sector: Automaker Criteria Assessment Table

**Automaker C1 — Companies Required to set Automaker Targets:** Companies whose emissions from manufacturing and lifecycle use of the following vehicles are more than 5% of the company's total scope 1, 2 and 3 emissions are considered to be automakers:

Cars and vans: 2-3 wheelers — all motorized vehicles having two or three wheels aimed at the mobility of persons on all types of roads. Light duty vehicles — all motorized vehicles having four wheels aimed at the mobility of persons on all types of roads, up to nine persons per vehicle and 3.5 tonnes (t) of gross vehicle weight.

Buses and trucks: Buses — buses (more than nine seats) and BRT systems (Bus Rapid Transit). Mini-buses. Medium freight trucks — commercial vehicles with a gross vehicle weight (GVW) from 3.5 t to 15 t; they include small lorries, rigid trucks, and tractor-trailers as well as large vans. Heavy freight trucks — commercial vehicles with a GVW greater than 15 t, they typically serve long-haul delivery of goods, have from two or more axles and a power rating of between 200 and 600 kW.

Companies that are considered to be automakers must set automaker targets that include 100% of scope 3 category 11 emissions at 1.5°C ambition, in line with criteria Automaker-C2 to C7.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **1.1 Appropriate activities** | Sector-Specific | Companies must set automaker targets if the GHG emissions corresponding to manufacturing and lifecycle use of their sold vehicles sum to equal to or greater than 5% of their total GHG emissions, where manufacturing and lifecycle emissions are defined as: Manufacturing emissions — all upstream cradle-to-gate emissions associated with the purchased & extracted materials and purchased services involved in manufacturing as well as all processing and production activities operated by the company or downstream of the company to produce the final vehicles. Lifecycle use of sold vehicles emissions — all well-to-wheel (WTW) emissions from the sold eligible vehicles' operation reported in scope 3 category 11. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Purchased goods and services / GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: S6113, S61113, S731, SAU1125, SAU1145. Provision of supporting documents displaying the emissions sources and the magnitude associated with the manufacturing and lifetime use of sold products emissions from sold vehicles. Confirmation reflecting accurate emissions coverage in the Targets section of the Validation Portal. |
| **1.2 Propulsion system GHG emissions accounting** | GHG Accounting | Companies selling fully assembled vehicles, engines or motors must account for the entire WTW GHG emissions associated with the energy consumed across their lifetime; the emissions must not be partially attributed to the manufacturer with weight-based allocation (such as relative to entire vehicle weight). | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products / GHG Inventory tab - Overview. Questions: S61113, S731. Provision of emissions breakdowns displaying the emissions sources and the magnitude associated with the lifetime use of sold products emissions from sold vehicles. |

**Automaker C2 — Target Boundary:** The SBTi Corporate Near-Term Criteria and Corporate Net-Zero Standard Criteria apply for scope 1 and 2 emissions and all scope 3 categories except for category 11. Automaker targets must cover 100% of use-phase emissions reported in scope 3 category 11 regardless of overall scope 3 coverage. Targets must cover the entire sales portfolio across the vehicle categories specified in Automaker-C1, without geographical exclusions. For use-phase emissions, the reporting boundary on a WTW basis must cover all operational modes including idling, repositioning and empty running, and add any other clarifications. Automakers shall report real world emissions and adjust test cycle emissions to reflect real emissions: Manufacturers are required to test the fuel consumption and corresponding emissions from the exhaust of newly produced vehicles using the Worldwide Harmonized Light Vehicle Test Procedure (WLTP) adjustment factors/formulas for passenger cars, vans, and light commercial vehicles (up to 3.5 t). Manufacturers are required to test the fuel consumption and corresponding emissions from the exhaust of newly produced vehicles using World Harmonized Heavy-Duty Certification (WHDC) adjustment factors/formulas for trucks, buses and coaches (over 3.5 t). Companies must use the adjustment factors/formulas of the Worldwide Harmonized Test Cycle (WLTC) to obtain real actual emissions.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **2.1 Appropriate emissions boundary for automaker targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting automaker targets must cover all direct scope 3 category 11 WTW GHG emissions from the lifetime use-phase of manufactured and sold: Cars and vans, Light duty vehicles, Buses, Mini-buses, Medium freight trucks, Heavy freight trucks. All emissions associated with the fuel or energy consumption of a sold vehicle are considered direct use-phase emissions, both the well-to-tank component and the tank-to-wheel component. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: S731, SAU1125, SAU1145. Confirmation and provision of all the required information. |
| **2.2 Appropriate activities for automaker targets** | Sector-Specific | Companies must have WTW emissions reported in category 11 from sold 2-3 Wheelers, Light duty vehicles, Buses, Mini-buses, Medium freight trucks, Heavy freight trucks to be eligible to set automaker targets, in which case they must report and cover 100% of these emissions with automaker targets. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: S61113, S731, SAU1125, SAU1145. Provision of all the required information. |
| **2.3 GHG Accounting Principles** | Sector-Specific | Companies must prioritise real world emissions reporting and apply explained and justified relevant adjustments to the relevant test cycle emissions determination where real world emissions data is not available. The relevant test cycles for each vehicle type are: Cars and vans - WLTP, Light duty vehicles - WLTP, Buses - WHDC, Mini-buses - WLTP, Medium freight trucks - WHDC, Heavy freight trucks - WHDC. The relevant adjustments are provided by the WLTP. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products. Questions: S61113. Provision of supporting documentation displaying the use of the relevant calculation methods on top of the relevant test cycle for determining real-world reflective use phase emissions of sold vehicles. |

**Automaker C3 — Well-to-Wheel Emissions (WTW) Coverage:** Calculation of GHG emissions for automakers' scope 3 category 11 targets shall be on a WTW basis.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **3.1 Well-to-Wheel emissions** | Target Setting | Companies setting automaker targets over scope 3 category 11 emissions from their sold eligible vehicles must report and target the lifetime transport activity emissions on a WTW basis. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products / GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: S61113, S731, SAU1125, SAU1145. Confirmation and breakdown of key scope 3 GHG emissions in each relevant category, alongside corresponding emissions magnitudes in the target tab of the Validation Portal. |
| **3.2 Lifetime WTW emissions calculations** | GHG Accounting | Companies setting automaker targets may use fuel mix and grid energy mix projections in the calculation of lifetime WTW GHG emissions, but any projections used must be clarified and justified with a commitment to rebaselining should actual mixes and projected mixes change significantly in subsequent years, influencing targeted emissions significantly. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Scope 3 - Use of sold products. Questions: S61113. Provision of supporting documents displaying recent trajectories in grid emissions intensities and fuel mix alongside other relevant metrics or information to justify the projections made and impacts on emissions calculations. |

**Automaker C4 — Target-Setting Method for Scope 3 Category 11:** Automakers must set absolute emission reduction targets for emissions for the use of sold products (scope 3 category 11) consistent with limiting warming to 1.5°C according to SBTi approved methods and pathways.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **4.1 Sufficient target ambition** | Target Setting | Companies setting automaker targets must set absolute reduction targets with ambition aligned with or exceeding the level of decarbonization required to keep global temperature increase well-below 1.5°C compared to pre-industrial temperatures. Please see NT C16 for further clarity on determination of this minimum ambition. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: SAU112191, SAU114191. Selection of the ambition aligned with or exceeding the level of decarbonization required to keep global temperature increase well-below 1.5°C compared to pre-industrial temperatures. |

**Automaker C5 — Expressing Absolute Targets in Intensity Terms:** Absolute automaker targets may be expressed in intensity terms (e.g. per unit sold) in the target language, but to do so, companies must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year unit sales and use those to calculate intensity reductions equivalent to the absolute target ambition. Companies setting automaker scope 3 category 11 targets must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year passenger-kilometers or metric tonne-kilometers of sold manufactured vehicles.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **5.1 Representative baseline for meaningful target ambition** | Target Setting | Companies setting automaker targets must ensure the base year chosen corresponds to WTW lifetime emissions and activity volumes that are representative of the organization's normal activities at the time of submission. Companies should avoid choosing base years where emissions magnitudes and the number of vehicles sales and corresponding lifetime usage are significantly different from those in surrounding years, because of the significant impacts of activity levels on resulting target year absolute emissions. Companies should return to the SBTi to recalculate targets if the targets are later determined to be calculated based on an unrepresentative or unsuitable base year. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - Overview / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: S741, SAU11214, SAU11414. Provision of supporting documents displaying recent trajectories in emissions, activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics to justify the choice of base year. Such relevant data for determining trends must be provided for at least 3 years. |
| **5.2 Disclosure of credible and justifiable activity projections** | Sector-Specific | Companies setting automaker targets and wishing to disclose the ambition in intensity terms must disclose credible and justifiable projected target year activity in terms of units sold, estimated lifetime metric tonne-kilometers or other suitable metric. The activity metric calculations must use consistent assumptions and calculation methods. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: SAU11211, SAU11213, SAU11214, SAU11411, SAU11413, SAU11414. Provision of supporting documents displaying that business planning and recent trajectories in activities, output, revenue or other relevant metrics result in the growth projections included in the Corporate Submission Form with regards to the automaker target. Such relevant data for determining trends must be provided for at least 3 years. |
| **5.3 Intensity target ambition** | Target Setting | The intensity target ambition used in the target language must be exactly equivalent to the absolute reduction target chosen by the company, which must follow Automaker C4 and C7 for minimum ambition requirements. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: SAU11219, SAU11419. Provision of supporting documents displaying that the growth projections included in determining the intensity reduction ambition result in equivalent absolute reduction to that targeted and stated in the Validation Portal. |
| **5.4 Inclusion of absolute reductions in target language** | Target Setting | Companies including intensity wording in the target language must also include the absolute reductions the target corresponds to in the target language. Target progress is assessed based on the absolute emissions regardless of emissions intensity equivalence stated in the target language. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: SAU11219, SAU112191, SAU11419, SAU114191. Confirmation of intended target language. |

**Automaker C6 — Phase Out of Internal Combustion Engines (ICE) Vehicles:** Car and van automakers setting science-based targets shall commit to work toward the phase out of new ICE cars and vans by 2035 in leading markets and by 2040 globally (or earlier as per local applicable regulation), and set interim targets consistent with this long-term goal. To demonstrate this commitment, car and van automakers must publish a statement alongside their science-based targets (and may demonstrate this commitment by, for example, signing the ZEV Declaration). The statement must follow the format, "Company X commits to [phase out / work toward the phase out of] new ICE cars and vans by 2035 in leading markets and by 2040 globally."

The statement must follow the format: "Company X commits to work toward the phase out of new internal combustion engine vehicles by 2035 in leading markets and by 2040 globally [or add earlier dates]."

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **6.1 ICE vehicle phase out commitment** | Sector Specific | Companies setting automaker targets must commit to phasing out ICE van and car production and/or sales by no later than 2040. | Portal Location: GHG Inventory tab - General questions / Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: S312, S313, SAU11222. Confirmation of business activities surrounding car and van production and/or sales alongside confirmation of target language adoption. |

**Automaker C7 — Near and Long-Term SBTi Tools:** Minimum ambition of near-term targets shall be calculated using the scope 3 tab in the SBTi Corporate Near-Term Tool, where WTW absolute emissions for the lifetime of vehicles sold in base year (entire portfolio) shall be entered. Minimum ambition of long-term targets shall be calculated in accordance with the SBTi's Corporate Net-Zero Standard Criteria using the Corporate Net-Zero Tool.

| Criteria Assessment Indicator | Applicability | Description | Minimum Documentation Required |
|-------------------------------|--------------|-------------|-------------------------------|
| **7.1 Automaker Target Ambition** | Target Setting | At a minimum, near-term scope automaker targets must be aligned with or exceed the level of absolute reduction decarbonization required to keep global temperature increase to 1.5°C compared to pre-industrial temperatures, according to the outputs of the Corporate Near-Term Target Setting Tool. | Portal Location: Targets tab - Add near-term sector specific target - Automakers / Targets tab - Add long-term sector specific target - Automakers. Questions: SAU11219, SAU112191, SAU11419, SAU114191. Confirmation of intended target ambition. |
